            d)'.

 480  0  
 481  0

 489  1  recode s26 s79 s81 s82 s250 s251 s252 s132
 490  1          (0=0)(1,2,3=1)(7777,8888,9999,-9999=sysmis)
 491  1    into cs26 cs79 cs81 cs82 cs250 cs251 cs252 cs132.
 492  1  
 493  1  recode s80 s83 (0,1=0) (2,3=1) (7777,8888,9999,-9999=sysmis)
 494  1   into cs80 cs83.
 495  1  
 496  1  if cs79 = 1 and cs80 = 1 cs79c = 1.
 497  1  if cs79 = 1 and cs80 = 0 cs79c = 0.
 498  1  if cs79 = 0 cs79c = 0.
 499  1  
 500  1  if cs82 = 1 and cs83 = 1 cs82c = 1.
 501  1  if cs82 = 1 and cs83 = 0 cs82c = 0.
 502  1  if cs82 = 0 cs82c = 0.
 503  1  
 504  1  if cs251 = 0 and cs252 = 0 cs251c = 0.
 505  1  if cs251 = 0 and cs252 = 1 cs251c = 1.
 506  1  if cs251 = 1 cs251c = 1.
 507  1  
 508  1  variable labels cs26 'use phone' cs79c 'cooking' cs81 'shopping 1' cs82c
 509  1   'shopping 2' cs250 'money/business' cs251c 'bills/cash' cs132 'medications'.
 510  1  value labels cs26 cs79c cs81 cs82c cs250 cs251c cs132 0 'no problems' 1
 511  1   'problems'.
 512  1  
 513  1  compute @func_sum = sum(cs26, cs79c, cs82c, cs250, cs251c, cs132).
 514  1  recode @func_sum (0,1,2 = 0) (-1=-1) (-2=-2) (3 thru hi=1) into @func_d.
 515  1  value labels @func_d 0 'zero(0), 1 or 2 problems' 1 '3+ problems'.
 516  1  var label @func_d 'Functional Impairment 3-point Scale for non-demented subjects (Manly)'.
 517  1  var label @func_sum  'Functional Impairment continuouse Scale for non-demented subjects (Manly)'.
 518  1  end if.
 519  1  
 520  1  ************ Memory Complaint Scale***************.
 521  1  
 522  0  do if (ccd01=0).
 523  0  
 524  1  recode s96 s92 s93a s93b s93c
 525  1          (0=0)(1=1)(7777,8888,9999,-9999=sysmis)
 526  1    into cs96 cs92 cs93a cs93b cs93c.
 527  1  
 528  1  variable labels cs96 'any memory difficulties'
 529  1                      /cs92 'any memory problem past month'
 530  1                      /cs93a 'memory for things read or heard'
 531  1                      /cs93b 'memory for names'
 532  1                     /cs93c 'remembering right word'.
 533  1  value labels cs96 cs92 cs93a cs93b cs93c 0 'no problems' 1 'problems'.
 534  1  
 535  1  recode d03 d05 d06 d07 (0=0) (5=1) (10= 1) into cd03 cd05 cd06 cd07.
 536  1  recode c1 c01 (0=0) (1=1) into cc1 cc01.
 537  1  compute memtsum = sum(cd03, cd05, cd06, cd07, cc1, cc01).
 538  1  
 539  1  compute mem_sum = sum(cs96, cs92, cs93a, cs93b, cs93c).
 540  1  
 541  1  compute mem_new = sum.1(mem_sum, memtsum).
 542  1  
 543  1  recode mem_new (0=0) (-1=-1) (-2=-2) (else = 1) into @mem_com.
 544  1  
 545  1  value labels @mem_com 0 'no complaints' 1 'any complaints'.
 546  1  var label @mem_com 'Memory Complaint Scale for non-demented subjects (Manly)'.
 547  1  
 548  1  end if.
 549  1  *freq @mem_com.
 550  1  
 551  1  
 552  1  ********CALCULATE T-SCORES****************************.
 553  1  
 554  0  do if (ccd01=0).
 555  0  
 556  0  *NOTE: The INTO code was added to the RECODE statement on Jan 2008 so that the original neuropsych
 557  0  *      variables would not be modified--the following compute variables are modified accordingly*.
 558  1  recode mem01 mem03 mem11 lan08 lan09 abs01 abs06 lan01 lan12 lan13 con01 con03
 559  1        (-1, -3 = sysmis) (-2 = 0)(else=copy)
 560  1   into mem01x mem03x mem11x lan08x lan09x abs01x abs06x lan01x lan12x lan13x con01x con03x.
 561  1  
 562  1  compute newmem = mean(mem01x, mem03x, mem11x).
 563  1  compute newabs = mean(lan08x, lan09x, abs01x, abs06x).
 564  1  compute newlan = mean(lan01x, lan12x, lan13x).
 565  1  compute newcon = mean(con01x, con03x).
 566  1  
 567  1  compute mem_p = (25.956 + (dem03 * 1.224) + (age_eval*-.146) + (dem06*.288) +
 568  1   (black*-1.406) + (hisp*-1.018)).
 569  1  compute mem_t = 50 + 10*((newmem - mem_p)/3.31428).
 570  1  
 571  1  compute abs_p = (15.950 + (age_eval*-.085) + (dem06*.418) + (black * -1.69) +
 572  1   (hisp*-1.562)).
 573  1  compute abs_t = 50 + 10*((newabs - abs_p)/2.43881).
 574  1  
 575  1  compute lan_p = (9.31 + (age_eval*-.011) + (dem06*.053) + (hisp*-.169)).
 576  1  compute lan_t = 50 + 10*((newlan - lan_p)/.65203).
 577  1  
 578  1  compute con_p = (6.948 + (dem03 * -.120) + (age_eval*-.024) + (dem06*.085) +
 579  1   (black*-.288) + (hisp*-.389)).
 580  1  compute con_t = 50 + 10*((newcon - con_p)/.82496).
 581  1  
 582  1  recode mem_t abs_t  lan_t  con_t (lowest through 34.9999 = 1) (35 through highest = 0)
 583  1   into memo_i abs_i  lan_i con_i.
 584  1  
 585  1  compute nmem_s = sum(abs_i, lan_i,  con_i).
 586  1  
 587  1  **NOTE: In Jan 2008 Manly code, labels are added to the following and
 588  1  **      these will be retained in the MULT files*.
 589  1  
 590  1  recode memo_i abs_i  lan_i con_i nmem_s (0=0) (1 through hi = 1) (sysmis
 591  1   = sysmis) into @mem_i @exec_i @lang_i @vspa_i nmem_i.
 592  1  
 593  1  var label @mem_i 'Memory composite from MCI criteria status (Manly)'
 594  1          @exec_i 'Executive function composite from MCI criteria status(Manly)'
 595  1          @lang_i 'Language function composite from MCI criteria status(Manly)'
 596  1          @vspa_i 'Visuospatial function composite from MCI criteria status(Manly)'.
 597  1  value label @mem_i @exec_i @lang_i @vspa_i  0 'normal' 1 'impaired'.
 598  1  
 599  1  end if.
 600  1  *freq @mem_i @exec_i @lang_i @vspa_i .
 601  1  
 602  1  **********define MCI groups********************************.
 603  1  **New code from Jennifer, January 2008*.
 604  1  
 605  1  *** Neuropsych only ********************************************************.
 606  0  do if ccd01=0.
 607  1  + if sum.4(@mem_i, @exec_i, @lang_i, @vspa_i)=0 @mcinp=0.
 608  1  + if any(1, @mem_i, @exec_i, @lang_i, @vspa_i)  @mcinp=1.
 609  1  
 610  1  + if sum.4(@mem_i, @exec_i, @lang_i, @vspa_i)=0 @memgpnp=0.
 611  1  + if any(1, @exec_i, @lang_i, @vspa_i)         @memgpnp=2.
 612  1  + if @mem_i=1                                @memgpnp=1.
 613  1  
 614  1  + compute nmsum = sum(@exec_i, @lang_i, @vspa_i).
 615  1  + if sum.4(@mem_i, @exec_i, @lang_i, @vspa_i)=0 @mci_gpnp=0.
 616  1  + if @mem_i=1                                @mci_gpnp=1.
 617  1  + if @exec_i=1                               @mci_gpnp=2.
 618  1  + if @lang_i=1                               @mci_gpnp=3.
 619  1  + if @vspa_i=1                               @mci_gpnp=4.
 620  1  + if @mem_i=1 & nmsum>=1                     @mci_gpnp=5.
 621  1  + if @mem_i=0 & nmsum>1                      @mci_gpnp=6.
 622  1  end if.
 623  1  
 624  0  var label @memgpnp  'Memory impairment subgroup using only MCI neuropsychological criteria (Manly)'
 625  0            @mcinp    'Meets neuropsychological criteria for MCI (Manly)'
 626  0            @mci_gpnp 'Cognitive impairment subgroups using only MCI neuropsychological criteria (Manly)'.
 627  0  
 628  0  value label
 629  0      @memgpnp  0 'Does not meet criteria'
 630  0          1 'Has memory impairment using only neuropsychological criteria'
 631  0          2 'Has impairment in one or more non-memory domains using only neuropsychological criteria'
 632  0     /@mcinp    0 'No' 1 'yes'
 633  0     /@mci_gpnp 0 'Does not meet criteria'
 634  0          1 'Has isolated memory impairment using only MCI neuropsychological criteria'
 635  0          2 'Has isolated executive impairment using only MCI neuropsychological criteria'
 636  0          3 'Has isolated language impairment using only MCI neuropsychological criteria'
 637  0          4 'Has isolated visuospatial impairment using only MCI neuropsychological criteria'
 638  0          5 'Has multi-domain impairment including memory using only MCI neuropsychological criteria'
 639  0          6 'Has non-memory multi-domain impairment using only MCI neuropsychological criteria'.
 640  0  
 641  0  *freq @memgpnp @mcinp @mci_gpnp.
 642  0  
 643  0  ************Petersen criteria  -  MCI subgroups***
 644  0  *New code from Jennifer, January 2008*.
 645  0
